*********************************************************************** 00020000
*                                                                     * 00030000
*  MACRO NAME:     /DISPLAY OUTPUT DSECTS                             * 00040000
*                                                                     * 00050000
*  STATUS:         IMS 12.1                                           * 00060000
*                                                                     * 00070000
*  FUNCTION:       DISPLAY DSECTS THAT MAP THE DISPLAY OUTPUT LINE    * 00080000
*                  FOR /DISPLAY COMMANDS.  ALL DISPLAY LINES MUST     * 00090000
*                  END WITH A X'15' NEWLINE CHARACTER.  HEADER LINES  * 00100000
*                  MUST HAVE AN ADDITIONAL NEWLINE CHARACTER AFTER    * 00110000
*                  THE LLZZ OF THE DISPLAY LINE.  THE CONVENTION      * 00120000
*                  FOR NUMBERING DISPLAY DSECT LINES FOLLOWS:         * 00130000
*                                                                     * 00140000
*                  X00-X49:  DISPLAY BODY LINE                        * 00150000
*                  X50-X69:  DISPLAY ERROR MESSAGE LINE               * 00160000
*                  X70-X79:  DISPLAY HEADER LINE                      * 00170000
*                                                                     * 00180000
*  EXAMPLE:        DISPLAY TYPE=B WILL EXPAND ALL OF THE DISPLAY      * 00190000
*                  DSECTS THAT BEGIN WITH B.                          * 00200000
*                                                                     * 00210000
* 05/01/03  ARS  UP9C01AS  V9R1  Forward fit to 9C                    * 00210100
* 03/12/07  mnz  PK42601   V101  /DIS AFFIN for MSC VGR               * 00210110
* 05/10/08  djr  PK70078   V10D  /DIS ACTIVE REG WAIT-CALLOUT         * 00210120
* 06/28/08  JR   PK70078   V10D  /DIS TMEM TPIPE SYNC                 * 00210130
* 07/31/08  djr  PK70078   V10D  /DIS ACTIVE REG TPIPE: tpipe         * 00210140
* 08/15/08  AV   PK68223   V101  CHANGE ELEM/ENTRY RATIO TO 5 DIGITS  * 00210150
* 10/09/08  djr  KB20029   V11A  FF of PK70078 & PK73539 to V11       * 00214150
* 03/30/09  JR   PK81543   V111  FF OF PK71135                        * 00214160
* 12/08/09  mnz  PM03085   V11   Remove TCP/IP NAME HDRS - FF PK85347 * 00214170
* 04/15/10  JCY  PM12142   V11   Display OTMA ICAL count      PM12142 * 00214180
* 04/15/10  SSC  PM05424   V11   ADD WID KEYWORD                      * 00214190
*--------------------------V12.1--------------------------------------* 00216000
* 02/19/09  SSC  UP12A1SC  V12A  CORRECT A67LEN                       * 00216010
* 07/15/09  jcy  U12VJY1   V121  Add ACEEAGE to /DIS OTMA             * 00216020
* 06/30/09  KQN  U12RKN1   V12R  /DIS OTMA, /DIS APPC AND /DIS ACTIVE * 00216030
* 04/30/10  KQN  KC30234   V12R  REMOVE OTMA IO TIMEOUT               * 00216040
* 01/14/10  djr  U12SDR1   V12S  Add SNAP OPT(DISPLAY) support        * 00216050
* 03/24/11  mnz  PM30305   V12S  Add PSTOPGEN to /DIS ASMT MSPLINK    * 00216060
*                                and GENIMSID to /DIS ACT             * 00216070
* 06/29/11  sls  PM40320   V12   OLC IN PROGRESS STATUS               * 00216080
* 10/28/11  BRM  PM33681   V12   Show tpipe count /DIS OTMA & TMEMBER * 00216090
*--------------------------V13.1--------------------------------------* 00217000
* 05/02/11  kqn  UP13GKN1  V13G  Add TCP6 Type                        * 00217010
* 08/11/11  rs   KD30016   V13A  Add A94 to /DIS A REGION             * 00217020
* 04/25/12  KQN  UP13GKN2  V13G  CHANGE TCP6 -> TCP                   * 00217030
* 05/25/12  djr  U13BDR1   V13B  Add y15nv constants                  * 00217040
* 07/19/12  jcy  UP13CJY1  V13C  TIB and INPT increase to 5 bytes     * 00217050
* 05/08/13  JCY  PM78756   V13   Add OTMA maxtp enhancement           * 00217060
* 08/01/13  ALJ  PM86117   V13   Add logger BSN & LSN in /DIS OLDS    * 00217070
*--------------------------V14.1--------------------------------------* 00218000
* 03/03/13  DC   U14BDC3   V14B  Add RTA to T60 & T97                 * 00218010
* 04/01/13  DC   U14BDC4   V14   MULTIRTP=Y OUTPUT DISPLAY T61        * 00218020

*********************************************************************** 00220000

*/*    X99:  /DISPLAY STANDARD TIMESTAMP MESSAGE                     */ 79190000
*/********************************************************************/ 79200000
*                                                                       79210000
*  DCL                                                                  79220000
*    1 X99        V,                   /* /DISPLAY standard             79230000
*                                         timestamp message          */ 79240000
*      3 X99LLZZ  CHAR(4),             /* LLZZ                       */ 79250000
*      3 X99FID   CHAR(3),             /* format ID = X99            */ 79260000
*      3 X99BLNK1 CHAR(1),             /* blank                      */ 79270000
*      3 X99TS    CHAR(0),             /* '*YYDDD/HHMMSS*' or           79280000
*                                         '*YYYYDDD/HHMMSS*'         */ 79290000
*      3 X99STAR1 CHAR(1),             /* '*'                        */ 79300000
*      3 X99DATE  CHAR(5),             /* 'XXXXX'                    */ 79310000
*      3 X99SLASH CHAR(1),             /* '/'                        */ 79320000
*      3 X99TIME  CHAR(6),             /* 'XXXXXX'                   */ 79330000
*      3 X99STAR2 CHAR(1),             /* '*'                        */ 79340000
*      3 X99NLC   CHAR(0),             /* new line character         */ 79350000
*      3 X99BLNK2 CHAR(2),             /* blanks                     */ 79360000
*      3 X99RSENM CHAR(8),             /* VTAM generic IMS APPL ID   */ 79370000
*      3 X99BLNK3 CHAR(2),             /* blanks                     */ 79380000
*      3 X99ACBAC CHAR(6),             /* 'ACTIVE' or 'BACKUP'       */ 79390000
*      3 X99DASH  CHAR(3),             /* ' - '                      */ 79400000
*      3 X99STATE CHAR(0);             /* one of the following:         79410000
*                                           'TRACKING'                  79420000
*                                           'INITIALIZATION'            79430000
*                                           'TAKEOVER IN PROGRESS'      79440000
*                                           'I/O TOLERATION'            79450000
*                                           'SYNCHRONIZING'          */ 79460000
*  DCL                                                                  79470000
*    1 * DEFINED(X99DATE),                                              79480000
*      3 X97DATE  CHAR(7),             /* 'YYYYDDD'                  */ 79490000
*      3 X97SLASH CHAR(1),             /* '/'                        */ 79500000
*      3 X97TIME  CHAR(6),             /* 'HHMMSS'                   */ 79510000
*      3 X97STAR2 CHAR(1),             /* '*'                        */ 79520000
*      3 X97NLC   CHAR(0),             /* new line character         */ 79530000
*      /**************************************************************/ 79540000
*      /* The following fields will be appended to the /DISLAY       */ 79550000
*      /* ACTIVE timestamp if the system is hotstandby capable.      */ 79560000
*      /**************************************************************/ 79570000
*      3 X97BLNK1 CHAR(2),             /* blanks                     */ 79580000
*      3 X97RSENM CHAR(8),             /* VTAM generic IMS APPL ID   */ 79590000
*      3 X97BLNK2 CHAR(2),             /* blanks                     */ 79600000
*      3 X97ACBAC CHAR(6),             /* 'ACTIVE' or "BACKUP'       */ 79610000
*      3 X97DASH  CHAR(3),             /* ' - '                      */ 79620000
*      3 X97STATE CHAR(0);             /* same choices as X99STATE   */ 79630000
*  DCL                                                                  79640000
*    X99ID    CHAR(3)   CONSTANT('X99'); /* format ID                */ 79650000
*                                                                       79660000
